### 1. 微缩人物模型生成：《剪刀老头》的日常生活

**Author**: [ハサミおじさん♪北海道のまちゼミ好きな二代目理容師](https://x.com/hasami_ojisan)  **Date**: 2026-01-17  **Language**: ja

> 此提示词可生成名为“剪刀老人”的角色进行各种日常活动的微缩模型。通过稍微修改提示词，用户可以想象该角色在不同场景中的样子，例如唱卡拉 OK、购物、阅读或使用电脑工作，这突显了输出内容的细节性和趣味性。

![微缩人物模型生成：《剪刀老头》的日常生活](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768717584637_skoj92_G-1xlUeaEAEj5tI.jpg)
![微缩人物模型生成：《剪刀老头》的日常生活](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768717584529_6dtbn2_G-1ximXaAAA48JP.jpg)
![微缩人物模型生成：《剪刀老头》的日常生活](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768717584780_xrt72e_G-1xn1VawAAzE-J.png)
![微缩人物模型生成：《剪刀老头》的日常生活](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768717586273_v3d0uq_G-1xpxzacAAfJkv.png)

```
ハサミおじさん のミニチュアフィギュアを4パターン作成！✨

🎤{argument name="活動1" default="一人カラオケ"} 🛒{argument name="活動2" default="スーパーで買い物"} 📖{argument name="活動3" default="読書"} 💻{argument name="活動4" default="PC作業"}

プロンプトを少し変えるだけで、おじさんの日常がこんなにリアルに具現化！このサイズ感とディテール、遊び心が止まりません(笑)
```

### 2. 用于 3D 建模的四视图角色参考图

**Author**: [Jennie](https://x.com/PurelyJennie)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: en

> 一个高度具体的提示，旨在为角色设计或 3D 建模目的，创建一名年轻成年女性的四视图参考图（正面、左侧面、右侧面、背面）。它要求采用纯白色背景和极简服装，以清晰展示详细的身体比例和肌肉线条。

![用于 3D 建模的四视图角色参考图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468610961_c2a45y_G-pSqcEawAADeXq.jpg)
![用于 3D 建模的四视图角色参考图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468611783_zia0py_G-pSpm2WEAAj7Wg.png)

```
Create a detailed and realistic full-body reference image on a plain white background, showing four views of the young adult woman in the attached image, follow this description:

    "body_description": 
      "ethnicity": "caucasian with fair skin tone"
      "hair": brown with blonde highlights, long, wavy",
      "build": "athletic hourglass, fit and toned",
      "torso": "narrow, high-waisted, plain stomach",
      "bust": "proportional, firm",
      "waist": "taut, slim, high-definition transition to hips",
      "hips": "wide, curvy, pronounced shelf-like curve at the iliac crest",
      "legs": "toned, athletic thighs with smooth skin transition",

Arrange the views horizontally from left to right: front view, left side profile view, right side profile view, and back view. In each pose, she stands straight with arms relaxed at her sides, feet slightly apart, wearing a simple black sports bra and black thong underwear to clearly display body proportions, muscle definition, facial details, hair, and posture. Ensure a 4:4 aspect ratio, high resolution, realistic rendering, no shadows, no additional elements, and equal spacing between views for easy reference.
```

### 8. Nano Banana Pro MBTI 人物形象可视化生成提示词

**Author**: [シュナプーン](https://x.com/schnapoon)  **Date**: 2025-12-30  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详尽图像生成提示，旨在将 MBTI 人格类型可视化为动漫风格的角色。它利用先前 LLM 分析得出的 MBTI 诊断结果（类型和原因），并用这些结果来定制一个基础角色档案（棕发红眼的动漫女孩）。该提示包含详细的 UI 布局说明（9:16 垂直图像，文本位置）、基于 16 种 MBTI 类型的角色分层规则（例如，ENTJ 获得军装夹克和皇冠），以及每个 MBTI 群体的特定颜色主题。

![Nano Banana Pro MBTI 人物形象可视化生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455062382_v5ky6k_G9YMqlCb0AAQ0jd.png)
![Nano Banana Pro MBTI 人物形象可视化生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455063584_p5r46e_G9YMyEfa8AAWWsv.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro MBTI 人物形象可视化生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455063856_v84bp3_G9YMq3PasAA-huH.jpg)

```
## 1. 入力変数 (ここを書き換えてください)
以下の情報を元にイラストを生成してください。

ユーザー情報:
target_account: "{argument name="アカウント名" default="@schnapoon"}"
mbti_type: {argument name="MBTIタイプ" default="ENTJ (指揮官型)"}
reason: "{argument name="診断理由" default="投稿はAIツールの活用法を構造的に共有し、ユーザーとの交流を積極的に行う。効率的なプロンプト作成と創造的アイデアの提案が目立ち、リーダーシップを発揮する思考パターンが見られる。"}"

キャラクター設定 (base_character_profile):
外見: アニメスタイルの少女。茶色のミディアムヘア、赤い瞳、少し尖った歯（ギザ歯）。

## 2. 生成指示書
A. 画像の全体構成 (UI Layout)
縦長 9:16の画像を生成してください。背景色は清潔感のあるオフホワイト（#F5F5F7）です。
画面は上から順に以下の要素で構成されます。

1.  ヘッダーテキスト:
       画面上部に `target_account` + " の診断結果は" というテキストを配置。
       色: ダークグレー (#333333)、フォントサイズ: 中、配置: 中央揃え。

2.  メインキャラクターイラスト:
       重要 (Consistency): `base_character_profile` の「身体的特徴（顔、髪、体型）」および「基本の服装（インナーやボトムスなど）」は変更せずに維持すること。
       変更点 (Layering): 基本服装の上から、下記の「B. MBTI別スタイル定義」で指定されたアウター、マント、装飾品などを「重ね着」させることでタイプごとの個性を表現すること。
       演出: キャラクターの周囲には指定されたエフェクトやフローティングアイテムを描画。
       スタイル: 高品質なアニメ塗り。

3.  MBTIタイプラベル:
       イラストの直下に `mbti_type` のテキストを大きく配置。
       色: 各タイプ定義のテーマカラー。
       フォント: 太字で視認性を高く。

4.  診断理由テキストボックス:
       画面下部に白い角丸のボックス（カード状のデザイン）を配置。
       その中に `reason` のテキストを日本語で記述。
       文字色: グレー (#555555)、左揃え、読みやすいサイズ。

B. MBTI別スタイル定義 (16 Types Layering Rules)
入力された `mbti_type` に合致するスタイルを適用し、基本服装の上に以下のアイテムを追加してください。

【分析家 (Analysts) - 紫/濃紺/深紅】
   INTJ (建築家):
       重ね着: 黒のロングコートまたは立ち襟のシックなジャケット。
       アイテム: チェス盤の駒、設計図のホログラム。
   INTP (論理学者):
       重ね着: 白衣（少し着崩している）、またはルーズなパーカー。
       アイテム: フラスコ、浮かぶ数式、ガジェット部品。
   ENTJ (指揮官):
       重ね着: 軍服風のナポレオンジャケット、または赤裏地の重厚なマント。
       アイテム: 指揮棒、王冠のような装飾。
   ENTP (討論者):
       重ね着: 奇抜なデザインのブレザー、またはマジシャンのようなケープ。
       アイテム: マイク、ニヤリとした表情、びっくり箱のようなエフェクト。

【外交官 (Diplomats) - 緑/金/パステル】
   INFJ (提唱者):
       重ね着: フード付きのローブ、または神秘的なショール。
       アイテム: ランタン、杖、神秘的な光の粒子。
   INFP (仲介者):
       重ね着: 大きめのニットカーディガン、または森ガール風のポンチョ。
       アイテム: 花冠、蝶々、本。
   ENFJ (主人公):
       重ね着: 英雄のようなマント、胸に輝くブローチやサッシュ（たすき）。
       アイテム: 聖剣（の形をした光）、後光のようなエフェクト。
   ENFP (広報運動家):
       重ね着: カラフルなパッチワークベスト、または派手なスカーフ。
       アイテム: 風船、紙吹雪、パーティーグッズ。

【番人 (Sentinels) - 青/白/ティール】
   ISTJ (管理者):
       重ね着: きっちりした紺のブレザー、腕章。
       アイテム: クリップボード、眼鏡、整列した書類。
   ISFJ (擁護者):
       重ね着: 清潔なエプロン、または医療用コート/ナース服風のアウター。
       アイテム: 救急箱、温かい飲み物（お茶など）。
   ESTJ (幹部):
       重ね着: フォーマルなスーツジャケット、
```

[[Character Design]] [[Anime Style]]

### 15. 根据照片制作的逼真角色设计图

**Author**: [Creative.Edge CL+](https://x.com/commonstyle)  **Date**: 2025-11-22  **Language**: ja

> 一个用于从照片生成电影级写实角色设计图的日文长提示词，包括多角度视图、表情图和姿势图，然后移除原始人物图像。

![根据照片制作的逼真角色设计图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763885585379_oiwknt_ruxtQefhmHdMJqYj.jpg)

```
この写真の人物の詳細なキャラクターデザインシートを作成してください。実写映画で使いますのでアニメの絵にならないように注意してください。必ず以下の3つのキャラクター設定で構成してください。作成できたら元の人物の画像は消してください。
 - キャラクターを複数の角度から描いたターンアラウンド（三面図）
 - 喜び、悲しみ、怒り、驚き、恐怖、中立など、基本的な感情状態がそれぞれ描かれた表情シート
 - キャラクターの走る、跳ぶ、笑う、泣くなどの典型的な行動を示したポーズシート
```

### 16. 超现实主义编辑肖像：墨水挽歌

**Author**: [timedoctor.eth](https://x.com/timedoctor_nft)  **Date**: 2026-03-01  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的提示，用于生成超现实主义的、超现实的编辑肖像。该提示指定了电影构图（三分法）、高对比度的明暗对照法照明，以及一种超现实的视觉呈现，其中主体的脸部被粘稠的黑色印度墨水和古董书法笔尖覆盖，模拟了实际效果。它针对特定的设备配置文件（哈苏 H6D-100c）和胶片模拟（柯达 Portra 800），以实现最大的真实感和氛围。

```
Ultra-premium minimalist still life photography of a single white porcelain espresso cup with a small right-side handle, filled with freshly extracted espresso that looks rich and delicious, featuring dense, velvety crema with a silky glossy surface, subtle natural swirl, golden-amber center fading into caramel-brown edges, fine micro-bubbles visible, warm and appetizing color depth. • proportions

• eye shape, spacing, stylization

• silhouette

• material identity

All soldiers are identical instances of the same character.
⚔️ Scene Concept & Motion Structure
The army transitions from formation into full charge:
• front rows breaking into aggressive motion

• mid rows reacting milliseconds later

• deeper rows still partially aligned
Motion spreads like a wave through the army
Each unit runs with controlled variation:
• different stride timing and body angles

• no identical poses

• all movement directed forward
Weapons:
• each unit carries an oversized medieval-style weapon

• designs vary but follow a unified visual language

• subtle controlled glow, never overpowering

• must not obscure character identity
🐉 Leader & Mount (COMMAND LAYER)
A commanding leader appears deeper in the frame, elevated above the formation:
• positioned off-center along a rule-of-thirds axis

• partially silhouetted through rain and haze

• clearly distinct from the soldiers through scale and placement
Mount Design Logic (CRITICAL):
• derived from the character’s material and world language

• no literal cloning or costume mimicry

• subtle harmony in form, texture, and accents
Pose:
• mount in forward surge, cutting through rain

• leader stable and controlled, not exaggerated

• presence communicates authority, not motion chaos
The leader has already moved.

The army is catching up.
🪂 Foreground Hero (IMPACT ANCHOR)
The closest instance dominates the foreground:
• captured mid-air in a dynamic jumping attack pose

• limbs extended with directional force

• weapon leading the motion
This figure acts as the visual entry point into the scene
🎥 Camera & Perspective (PRESSURE SHOT)
Ultra-low ground-level camera, almost touching wet terrain

18–24mm close-lens perspective
• foreground character enlarged by proximity

• army recedes diagonally into depth

• leader visible in mid/deep plane

• slight horizon tilt for instability

• some units cropped at frame edges
Viewer feels inside the charge
🔍 Depth of Field (MANDATORY)
Extremely shallow depth of field
• foreground hero = razor sharp

• nearby units slightly softened

• leader readable but partially diffused

• distant army dissolves into rain and haze
No full-frame clarity
💡 Lighting Doctrine (STORM LIGHT)
Hard directional back/side light cutting through rain
• strong rim light outlining silhouettes

• rain streaks illuminated as sharp lines

• deep shadow poc
```

[[Cinematic Lighting]]

### 68. 比较使用“宇宙女性”提示的图像模型

### 70. 电影级微距玩具摄影：冲刺中的角色

**Author**: [Edizkan ⭕🦇](https://x.com/edizkan_)  **Date**: 2026-03-17  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于使用 Nano Banana 2 生成电影级的微距玩具摄影场景，描绘一个来自上传参考图像的豆子大小的角色，在角色设计页面上爆发性地冲刺，强调精确的相似性保留和动态动作效果。

![电影级微距玩具摄影：冲刺中的角色](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773816076557_afodwy_HDly2BzX0AEdfxZ.jpg)

```
A cinematic macro toy-photography scene. A bean-sized version of the uploaded reference character is sprinting explosively captured at the peak stride moment of a high-speed sprint with visual effect. Character Pose: A dynamic, mid-sprint action pose with amazing visual effects captured from a three-quarter side profile. Torso: Leaning forward at a sharp angle to convey momentum. Arms: One arm is bent sharply at the elbow with the fist tucked near the chest; the other arm is extended backward, trailing behind the torso. Legs: In a full stride. The lead leg is bent forward with the knee high, while the trailing leg is fully extended back with the foot pointed. Head: Facing forward, aligned with the direction of the run. The character runs across the surface of several giant black-and-white character design pages fully covering the ground, featuring the same character. Likeness Preservation (CRITICAL): The identity of the character must remain exactly identical to the reference in both: • the miniature physical character • the character shown in the design sketches. The sketch pages must show the same character, including: • dynamic poses small sketches • head studies and shape explorations • proportion notes • accessory sketches • construction diagrams • small handwritten annotations. Maintain the exact: • head shape • eye shape and spacing • stylization • silhouette • materials and clothing design. If the character wears a balaclava, mask, helmet, or covered face, the sketches must not invent facial anatomy. No added nose. No added mouth. No visible skin where the reference does not show it. Do not humanize the character. Do not reinterpret anatomy. Subject & Action: The miniature character sprints explosively across the design pages, tearing through the sketch sheet as it runs. The character is captured at the peak stride moment of a full-speed sprint. Running pose details: • the body leans sharply forward as if accelerating • one leg is fully extended forward while the other drives powerfully backward • arms pump in opposite running motion • the torso twists slightly creating a dynamic curved spine line • the pose feels like a high-speed comic-book sprint. The character’s momentum rips through the paper, creating a jagged torn path behind it. A trail of torn paper curls and fragments with vfx follows behind the running character as if it burst out of its own design. Oversized design sheets surround the character, each page showing different stages of development of the same character. One small grey 3d print of the character is in the background as an exact copy of the uploaded image. Camera & Perspective: Captured from a medium camera distance above the desk, allowing a wider portion of the surrounding design pages to be visible. Shot with an 85mm macro lens, creating natural compression while keeping the environment readable. The camera sits slightly elevated and angled downward toward the running character. The character remains the focal point but occupies roughly one third of the frame, revealing more of the design sheets and workspace around it. The character remains slightly off-center within the spotlight. Depth of Field: Extremely shallow depth of field. The sprinting miniature character and the immediate section of the torn sketch page are razor sharp. Surrounding pages and distant elements fall into soft blur. Lighting (VERY DRAMATIC): A single narrow spotlight / flashlight beam hits the character. The beam comes from a side-front direction, creating a bright circular pool of light on the design page. Lighting characteristics: • extremely hard light • very high contrast • no ambient fill light • the surrounding elements fades into near-total darkness • sharp dramatic shadows stretch across the paper • edges of the light beam fall rapidly into black. The environment outside the spotlight should feel almost completely swallowed by darkness, as if the character has been suddenly caught under a stage light. Dust particles float through the beam. Environment & Surface Detail: Macro-level detail of the design pages: • ink texture • pencil strokes • paper fibers • subtle reflections on graphite lines. The torn paper edge reveals fibrous paper layers and curled fragments along the ripped path. Subtle Heat Burn Detail: Along parts of the torn path, the paper shows light scorching caused by extreme speed friction: • edges of some tears are slightly darkened and singed • faint burnt browning transitions into the white paper fibers • tiny ember-like glowing specks appear briefly along the freshest tear points • very subtle wisps of heat distortion or smoke rise from a few edges. The burn effect must remain minimal, believable, and physically grounded, enhancing realism without turning into flames or overpowering the scene. Color Grade: Desaturated sketch pages and environment. The character receives cool cinematic highlights from the spotlight. Moody macro photography atmosphere. Rendering Style: Photorealistic macro toy photography, emphasizing scale illusion between the tiny character and the giant design pages. Speed Energy VFX: A stylized high-speed energy trail follows behind the running character, emphasizing the explosive sprint. The trail consists of thin luminous motion streaks and glowing particles streaming backward from the character’s movement direction. Characteristics: • energy streaks originate from behind the character’s shoulders, arms, and legs • streaks extend diagonally backward, following the direction of motion • the lines are semi-transparent glowing blue light trails • small sparkling particles scatter along the trail • the effect should feel like comic-book speed energy, not smoke or fire • the VFX enhances motion but does not cover or obscure the character. The light streaks interact subtly with the environment: • faint glow reflecting on the torn paper edges • slight blue rim light on the character’s silhouette • a few glowing particles floating through the spotlight beam. The energy trail should feel fast, sharp, and directional, reinforcing the sense that the character is sprinting at extreme speed. ar 3:2
```

[[Cinematic Lighting]]

### 92. 时尚 Vlog 视频生成（Nano Banana Pro + Veo 3.1）

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-03-02  **Language**: ja

> 一个用于生成时尚视频博客的详细提示。图像首先使用 Nano Banana Pro 生成，然后使用 Google Veo 3.1 转换为视频。该提示侧重于电影般的画质、逼真的光线和自然的表情，最终呈现出一个简短的视频博客瞬间。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

```

```
{
  "prompt_type": "photorealistic suggestive indoor portrait",
  "main_composition": "low-angle full-body view of a single young woman squatting playfully in a modern bright home interior, knees bent wide apart with hands resting on thighs, teasing confident expression looking directly at camera with subtle pout and raised eyebrows, dynamic pose emphasizing curves and legs, bright natural indoor lighting with clean white cabinets and wooden floor in background",
  "subject": {
    "description": "beautiful young woman in her early 20s, attractive feminine features with light natural makeup (defined dark eyeliner, long lashes, subtle contour, glossy nude lips), large expressive eyes, fair smooth skin with healthy glow, long loose wavy blonde hair with natural volume falling over shoulders and slight tousle",
    "clothing": "fitted black long-sleeve mock-neck crop top or bodysuit with subtle stretch fabric ending at waist, paired with very short black high-cut shorts riding high on hips, sheer black pantyhose or tights with subtle opacity, completed with chunky black platform high-heeled shoes or loafers with thick soles",
    "details": "playful teasing expression with direct eye contact and faint pout, hair naturally wavy with soft strands framing face, manicured neutral nails visible on hands, confident relaxed pose with knees wide and slight forward lean creating dramatic leg emphasis"
  },
  "environment": {
    "foreground": "light wooden or laminate floor with subtle reflections",
    "midground": "woman centered in open space",
    "background": "modern bright home interior with white built-in cabinets or shelves containing books and decor, clean minimalist design with no clutter, subtle hallway or adjacent room visible"
  },
  "lighting_and_atmosphere": "bright even indoor daylight (likely from off-frame window) creating soft natural glow with warm highlights on skin, hair, black fabric sheen, and sheer pantyhose translucency, gentle shadows enhancing pose depth and curves, playful intimate casual vibe with high contrast between black outfit and light surroundings, photorealistic detail evoking teasing confidence",

**Author**: [Artificial intelligence (Ai),Open Ai](https://x.com/Vishnudxe)  **Date**: 2026-01-19  **Language**: en

> 一个全面的提示，旨在实现图像到图像的转换，指示 AI 将参考照片转换为高端电影风格的街头摄影肖像。它要求精确的面部特征应用，保留原始姿势，详细的服装增强（打蜡帆布派克大衣，靛蓝色牛仔裤），以及特定的电影照明（冷色调与暖金色边缘光），背景为历史悠久的塔楼，并带有强烈的焦外虚化效果。

![黄金时段街头肖像转换提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890689731_p1hr46_G_CFx8BXUAApWzb.jpg)

```
"Please use the female user’s reference photo to accurately apply all of her facial features. Edit this image — transform the photo into a high-end street-photography portrait of a female traveler/photographer leaning casually against a lamp post in front of a historic tower. Pose & composition (preserve): Standing with the left leg bent and foot resting on the lamp base, right leg relaxed. Left hand tucked into the jacket pocket, right hand holding a camera down by the thigh. Shoulders slightly turned toward the camera, chin gently lifted, gaze looking off-frame with a calm, confident expression. Keep the original framing and body alignment. Wardrobe & accessories: Keep the dark parka/jacket, enhance fabric texture with a subtle waxed canvas or premium matte finish Replace inner layer with a soft charcoal or muted knit sweater Retain blue jeans, deepen to rich indigo with natural creasing and realism Emphasize high-top sneakers — increase contrast on black-and-white panels, add light scuff details Add a slim messenger bag strap across the chest Add a compact leather wrist strap on the camera Optional: minimal jewelry (small studs or thin ring), understated and editorial Lighting & color grading: Cinematic cool-tone color grade with soft blue shadows. Add a warm golden rim light hitting the left side of the face and shoulder (late-afternoon sun feel). Slight contrast and midtone boost while preserving natural skin texture. Add subtle film grain and a gentle vignette to draw focus to the subject. Camera & optics look: Emulate a 35mm–50mm prime lens, shallow depth of field (f/1.8–2.8). The tower and pedestrians fall into smooth, painterly bokeh while the subject remains razor-sharp. Apply slight perspective correction so the tower peeks elegantly behind her shoulder. Enhance eye catchlights (or sunglasses reflection if present). Sharpen camera body and lens details. Background & atmosphere: Maintain the busy pedestrian environment but soften and desaturate it to make the subject pop. Increase clarity and texture on the historic stone tower for architectural strength. Add a few falling autumn leaves and a subtle wet-pavement sheen suggesting recent rain, with light reflections near the shoes. Final touches: Natural skin retouching (preserve pores and fine detail), boost micro-contrast on jacket and jeans, enhance glass and metal reflections on the camera. Export as photorealistic, vertical 4K editorial cro
```

### 184. 电影级工匠肖像提示词，适用于模型制作工坊

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-18  **Language**: en

> 这个详细的提示旨在生成一张电影风格的、国家地理式的肖像，描绘一位工匠正在制作一个著名建筑（如死星）的微缩模型。它详细说明了美学、材料、灯光和构图，以创造一个充满氛围的凌乱工作室的图像。

![电影级工匠肖像提示词，适用于模型制作工坊](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804200756_qsy04i_G-qqqVqW0AEDVtg.jpg)
![电影级工匠肖像提示词，适用于模型制作工坊](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804202314_562r8e_G-qqqVqWYAAYl87.jpg)

```
Do this for {argument name="structure name" default="Death Star"}: <instruction>
  1. The Semantic Inference Engine (The Masterpiece):  
Input A is a Famous Building, City, or Fictional Structure (e.g., The Colosseum, Hogwarts, The Death Star).
Analyze the subject to determine the   Model Aesthetic  :
   The Material:  Identify the primary modeling medium.
   (e.g., Ancient Ruins -> Plaster/Clay. Modern City -> White Foamcore/Acrylic. Fantasy -> Wood/Moss). 
   The Blueprints:  Identify the reference documents on the table.
   (e.g., Vintage Parchment Maps vs. Blue Cyanotypes vs. Digital CAD printouts). 
2.  The Workshop :
Goal: "Cinematic Artisan" Portrait.
The Room: A cluttered, high-ceilinged Model Maker's Studio. Wooden shelves line the walls, filled with "Previous Projects" (other models in the same genre).
The Character: an input inspired maker character wearing a relevant apron and an appropriate Visor or protective tool
The Table: A scarred wooden workbench covered in scale modeling tools: X-Acto knives, glue bottles, sanding blocks, and sawdust.
3. The Narrative :
The Pose: The craftsman is leaning in close to the "Model" (Input A), which sits centrally on the table.
The Interaction: He is delicately placing a Tiny Detail Component onto the structure using tweezers or his fingers.
(e.g., Planting a miniature tree, placing a tiny flag, or gluing a microscopic figure).
The Scale: The model looks grand but miniature; the human hands look massive and weathered in comparison.
4. Lighting & Atmosphere:
Lighting: Volumetric God Rays (Tyndall Effect). A strong, singular shaft of warm sunlight streams in from a high window (top left/center), illuminating the floating dust particles and spotlighting the model.
Contrast: The workshop corners are in deep shadow; the work surface is bright.
Palette: Warm, dusty Earth Tones (Browns, Golds, Beiges).
Output: ONE image, 16:9 Aspect Ratio, Cinematic Photography, "National Geographic" aesthetic, Volumetric Lighting.
</instruction>
```

### 199. 超现实披萨风景和赛博朋克汽车

**Author**: [Taaruk](https://x.com/Taaruk_)  **Date**: 2026-01-11  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的 JSON 提示，用于生成一个超现实、超详细的奇幻世界，其中披萨元素融入了景观和技术。它概述了两个截然不同的场景：一条由意大利辣香肠披萨制成的沿海山路，以及一辆由披萨片制成的未来赛博朋克汽车，强调了逼真的食物纹理和电影风格。

![超现实披萨风景和赛博朋克汽车](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768226052590_avjzoi_G-Yy_EDaMAAcq0S.jpg)

![超现实披萨风景和赛博朋克汽车](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768226054059_8nlj4o_G-Yy_H3bIAAaSQT.jpg)

        }
      },

      },

    },

      },
